Hello,
I've added some features to Authen::Captcha that I thought I'd share  
back but I can't contact the author, Joshua L. Miller.  If you can  
kindly fwd my thanks and the modified code to him, I'd much appreciate  
it.

The changes are:
1.  The index keys and images can now be stored into a database table  
instead of a flat-file.  This was because I needed to use your code on  
a website that was load-balanced across multiple servers and I wanted  
to avoid lock issues with NFS mounts.
2. For extra security, I added a user-defined secret key to add to the  
code when generating the md5sum.

And also to access the images from the database from an Apache based  
server, I created Authen::Captcha::Apache that holds the handler for  
retrieving the image from the database and delivering it as a normal  
png.

I've amended the documentation with my changes.

I've attached the code changes.  It's the actual source code without  
makefiles and such.

Cheers,
Himmy

--Apple-Mail-20--530003575
